b.meta.MinTime:\\n246: \\t\\t\\treturn -1\\n247: \\t\\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\\n248: \\t\\t\\treturn 1\\n249: \\t\\tdefault:\\n250: \\t\\t\\treturn 0\\n251: \\t\\t}\\n252: \\t})\\n253: \\n254: \\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\\n255: \\tif len(res) > 0 {\\n256: \\t\\treturn res, nil\\n257: \\t}\\n258: \\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\\n259: \\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\\n260: \\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\\n261: \\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\\n262: \\n263: \\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\\n264: \\t\\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\\n265: \\t}\\n266: \\tif len(res) > 0 {\\n267: \\t\\treturn res, nil\\n268: \\t}\\n269: \\n270: \\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\\n271: \\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\\n272: \\t\\tmeta := dms[i].meta\\n273: \\t\\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\\n274: \\t\\t\\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\\n275: \\t\\t\\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\\n276: \\t\\t\\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\\n277: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\\n278: \\t\\t\\t}\\n279: \\t\\t\\tbreak\\n280: \\t\\t}\\n281: \\t\\tif \\n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\\n292: \\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\\n293: \\t\\treturn nil\\n294: \\t}\\n295: \\n296: \\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\\n297: \\n298: \\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\\n299: \\t\\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\\n300: \\t\\tif len(parts) == 0 {\\n301: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n302: \\t\\t}\\n303: \\n304: \\tOuter:\\n305: \\t\\tfor _, p := range parts {\\n306: \\t\\t\\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\\n307: \\t\\t\\tfor _, dm := range p {\\n308: \\t\\t\\t\\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\\n309: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tcontinue Outer\\n310: \\t\\t\\t\\t}\\n311: \\t\\t\\t}\\n312: \\n313: \\t\\t\\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\\n314: \\t\\t\\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\\n315: \\t\\t\\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\\n316: \\t\\t\\t// or is before the most recent block.\\n317: \\t\\t\\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\\n318: \\t\\t\\t// size still fits in the range.\\n319: \\t\\t\\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\\n320: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn p\\n321: \\t\\t\\t}\\n322: \\t\\t}\\n323: \\t}\\n324: \\n325: \\treturn nil\\n326: }\\n327: \\n328: // selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\\n329: // It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\\n330: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\\n331: \\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\\n332: \\t\\treturn nil\\n333: \\t}\\n334: \\tif len(ds) < 2 {\\n335: \\t\\treturn nil\\n336: \\t}\\n337: \\tvar overlappingDirs []string\\n338: \\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\\n339: \\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\\n340: \\t\\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\\n341: \\t\\t\\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\\n342: \\t\\t\\t\\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\\n343: \\t\\t\\t}\\n344: \\t\\t\\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\\n345: \\t\\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\\n346: \\t\\t\\tbreak\\n347: \\t\\t}\\n348: \\t\\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\\n349: \\t\\t\\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\\n350: \\t\\t}\\n351: \\t}\\n352: \\treturn overlappingDirs\\n353: }\\n354: \\n355: // splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\\n356: //\\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\\n360: \\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\\n361: \\n362: \\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\\n363: \\t\\tvar (\\n364: \\t\\t\\tgroup []dirMeta\\n365: \\t\\t\\tt0    int64\\n366: \\t\\t\\tm     = ds[i].meta\\n367: \\t\\t)\\n368: \\t\\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\\n369: \\t\\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\\n370: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\\n371: \\t\\t} else {\\n372: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\\n373: \\t\\t}\\n374: \\t\\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\\n375: \\t\\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\\n376: \\t\\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n377: \\t\\t\\ti++\\n378: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n379: \\t\\t}\\n380: \\n381: \\t\\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\\n382: \\t\\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\\n383: \\t\\t\\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\\n384: \\t\\t\\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n385: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n386: \\t\\t\\t}\\n387: \\t\\t\\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\\n388: \\t\\t}\\n389: \\n390: \\t\\tif len(group) > 0 {\\n391: \\t\\t\\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\\n392: \\t\\t}\\n393: \\t}\\n394: \\n395: \\treturn splitDirs\\n396: }\\n397: \\n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. \\t\\t}\\n422: \\t\\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\\n423: \\t\\t\\tULID:    b.ULID,\\n424: \\t\\t\\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\\n425: \\t\\t\\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\\n426: \\n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\\n292: \\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\\n293: \\t\\treturn nil\\n294: \\t}\\n295: \\n296: \\thighTime := \\t\\t}\\n303: \\n304: \\tOuter:\\n305: \\t\\tfor _, p := range parts {\\n306: \\t\\t\\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\\n307: \\t\\t\\tfor _, dm := range p {\\n308: \\t\\t\\t\\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\\n309: \\t\\t\\t\\t\\tcontinue Outer\\n310: \\t\\t\\t\\t}\\n311: \\t\\t\\t}\\n312: \\n313: \\t\\t\\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\\n314: \\t\\t\\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\\n315: \\t\\t\\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\\n316: \\t\\t\\t// or is before the most recent block.\\n317: \\t\\t\\t// {\\n331: \\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\\n332: \\t\\treturn nil\\n333: \\t}\\n334: \\tif len(ds) < 2 {\\n335: \\t\\treturn nil\\n336: \\t}\\n337: \\tvar overlappingDirs []string\\n338: \\t}\\n352: \\treturn overlappingDirs\\n353: }\\n354: \\n355: // splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\\n356: //\\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\\n360: \\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\\n361: \\n362: \\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\\n363: \\t\\tvar (\\n364: \\t\\t\\tgroup []dirMeta\\n365: \\t\\t\\tt0    int64\\n366: \\t\\t\\tm     = ds[i].meta\\n367: \\t\\t)\\n368: \\t\\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\\n369: \\t\\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\\n370: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\\n371: \\t\\t} else {\\n372: \\t\\t\\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\\n373: \\t\\t}\\n374: \\t\\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\\n375: \\t\\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\\n376: \\t\\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n377: \\t\\t\\ti++\\n378: \\t\\t\\tcontinue\\n379: \\t\\t}\\n380: \\n381: \\t\\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\\n382: \\t\\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\\n383: \\t\\t\\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\\n384: \\t\\t\\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\\n385: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n386: \\t\\t\\t}\\n387: \\t\\t\\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\\n388: \\t\\t}\\n389: \\n390: \\t\\tif len(group) > 0 {\\n391: \\t\\t\\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\\n392: \\t\\t}\\n393: \\t}\\n394: \\n395: \\treturn splitDirs\\n396: }\\n397: \\n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. \\t\\t}\\n422: \\t\\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\\n423: \\t\\t\\tULID:    b.ULID,\\n424: \\t\\t\\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\\n425: \\t\\t\\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\\n426: c.plan(dms)\n240: }\n241: \n242: func (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n243: \tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n244: \t\tswitch {\n245: \t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n246: \t\t\treturn -1\n247: \t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n248: \t\t\treturn 1\n249: \t\tdefault:\n250: \t\t\treturn 0\n251: \t\t}\n252: \t})\n253: \n254: \tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n255: \tif len(res) > 0 {\n256: \t\treturn res, nil\n257: \t}\n258: \t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n259: \t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n260: \t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n261: \tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n262: \n263: \tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n264: \t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n265: \t}\n266: \tif len(res) > 0 {\n267: \t\treturn res, nil\n268: \t}\n269: \n270: \t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n271: \tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n272: \t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n273: \t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n274: \t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n275: \t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n276: \t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n277: \t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n278: \t\t\t}\n279: \t\t\tbreak\n280: \t\t}\n281: \t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n282: \t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n283: \t\t}\n284: \t}\n285: \n286: \treturn nil, nil\n287: }\n288: \n289: // selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n290: // If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\n291: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n292: \tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n293: \t\treturn nil\n294: \t}\n295: \n296: \thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n297: \n298: \tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n299: \t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n300: \t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n301: \t\t\tcontinue\n302: \t\t}\n303: \n304: \tOuter:\n305: \t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n306: \t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n307: \t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n308: \t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n309: \t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n310: \t\t\t\t}\n311: \t\t\t}\n312: \n313: \t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n314: \t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n315: \t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n316: \t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n317: \t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n318: \t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n319: \t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n320: \t\t\t\treturn p\n321: \t\t\t}\n322: \t\t}\n323: \t}\n324: \n325: \treturn nil\n326: }\n327: \n328: // selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n329: // It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\n330: func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n331: \tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n332: \t\treturn nil\n333: \t}\n334: \tif len(ds) < 2 {\n335: \t\treturn nil\n336: \t}\n337: \tvar overlappingDirs []string\n338: \tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n339: \tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n340: \t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n341: \t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n342: \t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n343: \t\t\t}\n344: \t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n345: \t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n346: \t\t\tbreak\n347: \t\t}\n348: \t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n349: \t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n350: \t\t}\n351: \t}\n352: \treturn overlappingDirs\n353: }\n354: \n355: // splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n356: //\n357: // For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n358: // it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\n359: func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n360: \tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n361: \n362: \tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n363: \t\tvar (\n364: \t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n365: \t\t\tt0    int64\n366: \t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n367: \t\t)\n368: \t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n369: \t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n370: \t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n371: \t\t} else {\n372: \t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n373: \t\t}\n374: \t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n375: \t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n376: \t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n377: \t\t\ti++\n378: \t\t\tcontinue\n379: \t\t}\n380: \n381: \t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n382: \t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n383: \t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n384: \t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n385: \t\t\t\tbreak\n386: \t\t\t}\n387: \t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n388: \t\t}\n389: \n390: \t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n391: \t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n392: \t\t}\n393: \t}\n394: \n395: \treturn splitDirs\n396: }\n397: \n398: // CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n399: // and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\n400: func CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n401: \tres := &BlockMeta{\n402: \t\tULID: uid,\n403: We need to lock the reload to avoid the situation where\n1436: \t// a normal reload and CleanTombstones try to delete the same block.\n1437: \tdb.mtx.Lock()\n1438: \tdefer db.mtx.Unlock()\n1439: \n1440: \tloadable, corrupted, err := openBlocks(db.logger, db.dir, db.blocks, db.chunkPool)\n1441: \tif err != nil {\n1442: \t\treturn err\n1443: \t}\n1444: \n1445: \tdeletableULIDs := db.blocksToDelete(loadable)\n1446: \tdeletable := make(map[ulid.ULID]*Block, len(deletableULIDs))\n1447: \n1448: \t// Mark all parents of loaded blocks as deletable (no matter if they exists). {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Nq8SrWmhMoWXr2VYSnYPhh","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_012AeqVgVn4t41hv4d8gnbeV","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What is TSDB Compaction?\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction in Prometheus is the process of merging and optimizing disk-based time series blocks. As Prometheus ingests data, the in-memory \"Head\" block accumulates samples. When the Head reaches a configured time threshold (default: 2 hours), it is persisted to disk as a new block. Compaction then:\n\n1. **Merges overlapping blocks** into larger, more efficient blocks\n2. **Removes tombstoned (deleted) series** from blocks\n3. **Reorganizes data** to improve query performance\n4. **Manages disk space** by consolidating multiple small blocks into fewer larger ones\n\n### Block Structure and Levels\n\nPrometheus uses a **leveled compaction strategy**:\n\n- **Level 0**: Head blocks persisted from in-memory data (time range: typically 2 hours)\n- **Level 1+**: Progressively larger blocks created by merging smaller blocks\n\nBlock ranges grow exponentially (e.g., 2h → 10h → 50h → 250h) to maintain balanced query performance and retention efficiency.\n\n### When Compaction Is Triggered\n\nCompaction is initiated in two ways:\n\n#### 1. Time-Based (Periodic, Primary)\n- **Trigger**: Every 1 minute, the background compaction loop (`tsdb/db.go:995`) checks if the Head is compactable\n- **Condition**: Head block age ≥ half of configured `MinBlockDuration` (default: 1 hour)\n- **Code reference**: `tsdb/db.go:1162-1188`\n\n#### 2. Sample-Based (Append-Time, Secondary)\n- **Trigger**: When appenders commit samples after Head becomes \"compactable\"\n- **Condition**: Head block time range exceeds threshold\n- **Code reference**: `tsdb/db.go:1115-1127` (dbAppender.Commit)\n\n#### 3. Tombstone-Based (Cleanup)\n- **Trigger**: When a block has >5% tombstones OR all samples are deleted\n- **Condition**: Automatic selection during Plan phase\n- **Code reference**: `tsdb/compact.go:270-284`\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\n#### **Compaction Execution Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total number of completed compactions | Increasing—should increment regularly |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions attempted (may fail) | Should track with `compactions_total` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Number of failed compaction attempts | **Alert if > 0 in 1h** |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Compactions skipped (auto-compaction disabled) | Monitor; expected if compaction is disabled |\n\n#### **Compaction Duration and Performance**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Wall-clock time to complete compaction | **Alert if p99 > block_range** |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Final chunk sizes during compaction | Monitor for anomalies in distribution |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk after compaction | Monitor; indicates compression efficiency |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time range of chunks post-compaction | Monitor for fragmentation |\n\n#### **Vertical (Overlapping) Compaction**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block merges | Monitor for frequency; high frequency = many overlaps |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | 1 if block is being written, 0 otherwise | **Alert if stuck at 1 for > 5min** |\n\n#### **Block and Retention Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of currently loaded blocks | Increasing = blocks not being deleted |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total disk space used by blocks | Monitor for exceeding max disk capacity |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max bytes to retain | Compare with `storage_blocks_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds` | Gauge | Configured retention duration (seconds) | Reference for time-based cleanup |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted by time-based retention | Increasing = old blocks cleaned up |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted by size-based retention | Increasing = disk limit enforced |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to clean tombstones from blocks | Monitor for unusual delays |\n\n### Sample Alert Rules\n\n```yaml\n# High-severity: Compaction is failing\n- alert: TSDBCompactionFailures\n  expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[1h]) > 0\n  for: 5m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB compaction failing on {{ $labels.instance }}\"\n    description: \"{{ $value }} compaction failures in the last hour\"\n\n# Medium-severity: Compaction is slower than block range\n- alert: TSDBCompactionSlowdown\n  expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > on(instance) prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds / 24\n  for: 10m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB compaction is taking too long on {{ $labels.instance }}\"\n\n# Medium-severity: Block population is stuck\n- alert: TSDBBlockPopulatingStuck\n  expr: prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n  for: 5m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB block population stuck on {{ $labels.instance }}\"\n\n# High-severity: Disk space exhaustion imminent\n- alert: TSDBStorageNearLimit\n  expr: prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes > 0.9\n  for: 5m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB storage is at {{ $value | humanizePercentage }} of configured limit\"\n```\n\n### Distinguishing Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Healthy Compaction Indicators:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` incrementing every 1-10 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` < block time range (e.g., < 2h for 2h blocks)\n- No increase in `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` cycles between 1 and 0 (not stuck at 1)\n\n**Stuck Compaction Indicators:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` = 1 for > 5 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` increasing without completion\n- Error logs: \"compaction failed\" with increasing frequency (backoff grows: 1s → 2s → 4s → ... → 1m)\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes and Diagnostics\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Logs: `Failed to write 'Deletable' to meta file after compaction` or `remove tmp folder after failed compaction: no space left on device`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` reaches or exceeds `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes`\n- New samples rejected with I/O errors\n- Prometheus unable to create new blocks\n\n**Root Cause:**\n- Compaction requires temporary disk space to write the new merged block before deleting source blocks\n- If available free space < new block size, the write fails\n- Retention cleanup not keeping pace with ingestion rate\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check disk usage:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /prometheus-data/\n   du -sh /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n   ```\n\n2. Check current block sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data/tsdb/ | head -50\n   ```\n\n3. Examine Prometheus metrics:\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\n   ```\n\n4. Review logs for specific error:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"compaction\\|disk\\|space\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -100\n   ```\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction write failure: `tsdb/compact.go:606-718` (write function)\n- Temporary file handling: `tsdb/db.go:1133-1212` (Compact method)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` continuously increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` not incrementing\n- Logs show backoff: \"compaction failed\" errors with exponential wait times (1s, 2s, 4s, ..., 60s)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1\n- Queries slow down due to many small blocks being queried\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` high and increasing\n\n**Root Cause:**\n- Failed block opens during compaction (corrupted metadata)\n- Mutex/locking contention during reloadBlocks\n- Insufficient memory for merging large blocks\n- Compaction plan selects blocks with `Failed` flag (prevents further compaction)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check compaction error messages:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"failed\\|panic\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n2. Verify block integrity:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data/tsdb/ 2>&1 | grep -i \"failed\\|corrupt\\|error\"\n   ```\n\n3. List blocks and check for `Failed` status:\n   ```bash\n   ls -la /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n   for block in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     echo \"=== $block ===\"\n     jq '.compaction.failed' \"$block\"\n   done\n   ```\n\n4. Monitor block loading during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   watch -n 1 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded'\n   ```\n\n5. Check for \"reloadBlocks\" errors in logs:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"reloadBlocks\\|reload blocks\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Backoff logic: `tsdb/db.go:982-1027` (run loop with exponential backoff)\n- Compaction with failure detection: `tsdb/compact.go:305-310` (selectDirs skips blocks with Failed flag)\n- Block opening: `tsdb/compact.go:444-487` (Compact method)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Logs: `Corrupted block` or `open index reader for block ... error`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Specific blocks in `/prometheus-data/tsdb/` listed as corrupted\n- Queries fail with \"block not found\" or index read errors\n- Prometheus startup slow (repairing WAL/WBL during init)\n\n**Root Cause:**\n- Incomplete block writes (Prometheus crash during compaction)\n- Disk corruption (bitflips, filesystem errors)\n- Incompatible index/chunk format after upgrades\n- Orphaned blocks from failed compaction with temporary directory not cleaned up\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Identify corrupted blocks:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"corrupted block\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -o \"[a-z0-9]\\{26\\}\"\n   ```\n\n2. Inspect block metadata:\n   ```bash\n   # For each problematic ULID:\n   jq . /prometheus-data/tsdb/{ULID}/meta.json\n   ```\n\n3. Check block compaction status:\n   ```bash\n   jq '.compaction' /prometheus-data/tsdb/{ULID}/meta.json\n   ```\n\n4. Validate block with promtool:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /prometheus-data/tsdb/{ULID} > /tmp/dump.txt 2>&1\n   head -20 /tmp/dump.txt  # Check for errors\n   ```\n\n5. Review startup logs for WAL repair:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"repair\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Corruption detection: `tsdb/db.go:1440-1478` (reloadBlocks detects corrupted blocks)\n- Block opening with error handling: `tsdb/compact.go:475-481`\n- WAL repair on startup: `tsdb/db.go:918-933`\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Logs: `fatal error: runtime: out of memory`\n- Process receives SIGKILL or OOM killer signal\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1 before crashing\n- Memory usage spikes during compaction and never released\n- System load increases dramatically during failed compaction attempt\n\n**Root Cause:**\n- Block series count too high for available memory\n- Memory not released after closing block readers\n- Chunk pool exhaustion (too many chunks in flight)\n- Symbol table or index reader holding excessive memory\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Monitor memory usage during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   # Before triggering compaction, start monitoring:\n   watch -n 0.5 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep | awk \"{print \\$6}\"'\n\n   # Or use Go metrics (requires pprof):\n   curl http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/heap > /tmp/heap.prof\n   go tool pprof /tmp/heap.prof\n   (pprof) top10  # Show top memory consumers\n   ```\n\n2. Check configured memory limits:\n   ```bash\n   # Check cgroup limits (container/Kubernetes):\n   cat /sys/fs/cgroup/memory/memory.limit_in_bytes\n\n   # Check Prometheus flags:\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -o \"\\-\\-storage.*\"\n   ```\n\n3. Examine block sizes before compaction:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data/tsdb/ | head -20\n   # Look for blocks with high series/chunk counts\n   ```\n\n4. Review logs for memory warnings:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"memory\\|heap\\|gc\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Memory allocation during compaction: `tsdb/compact.go:729-875` (PopulateBlock)\n- Chunk pool management: `tsdb/compact.go:77-87` (LeveledCompactor with chunkPool)\n- Symbol iteration: `tsdb/compact.go:803-810`\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery Procedure 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Objective:** Free disk space so compaction can resume and proceed normally.\n\n**Steps:**\n\n1. **Assess the situation** (2 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Check available space\n   df -h /prometheus-data/\n\n   # Get current block usage\n   du -sh /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n\n   # Get configured retention\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit\n   ```\n\n2. **Option A: Reduce retention period** (5 minutes, fastest):\n\n   a. Stop Prometheus:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n   b. Edit Prometheus config to reduce `--storage.tsdb.retention.time`:\n   ```bash\n   # Current: e.g., 30 days\n   # Reduce to: e.g., 7 days\n   vi /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n   ```\n\n   c. Start Prometheus (it will cleanup old blocks on startup):\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Monitor cleanup:\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"retention\"\n   ```\n\n   d. Verify recovery:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /prometheus-data/\n   # Should show freed space within 2 minutes\n   ```\n\n3. **Option B: Manual block deletion** (if Option A is insufficient):\n\n   a. List blocks by age:\n   ```bash\n   ls -ltr /prometheus-data/tsdb/ | tail -20\n   ```\n\n   b. Identify and delete old blocks (keep at least 3 recent blocks):\n   ```bash\n   # List all blocks with their max time\n   for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/; do\n     maxtime=$(jq .maxTime \"$d/meta.json\" 2>/dev/null)\n     echo \"$(basename $d): $maxtime\"\n   done | sort -t: -k2 -n\n\n   # Delete blocks older than X (be cautious)\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/tsdb/{OLDEST_ULID}/\n   ```\n\n   c. Restart Prometheus to re-index:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor compaction resumption** (5-10 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for compaction progress\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | \\\n     grep \"prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\\|prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes\"'\n\n   # Should see:\n   # - prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total increasing\n   # - prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes decreasing\n   ```\n\n5. **Verify health** (2 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Check for new failures\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep compactions_failed\n   # Should NOT increase after recovery\n\n   # Check disk space\n   df -h /prometheus-data/\n   # Should show adequate free space (>20% of volume recommended)\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Set `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` with 30% buffer headroom\n- Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` and alert at 80% of limit\n- Schedule regular reviews of retention policy\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Objective:** Unblock compaction by removing failed blocks or restarting the service.\n\n**Steps:**\n\n1. **Identify the root cause** (5 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Check for failed blocks in metadata\n   for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     failed=$(jq '.compaction.failed' \"$d\" 2>/dev/null)\n     if [ \"$failed\" = \"true\" ]; then\n       echo \"Failed block: $(dirname $d)\"\n     fi\n   done\n\n   # Check for specific errors\n   grep -i \"failed\\|corrupt\\|panic\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -20\n   ```\n\n2. **If failed blocks exist, clear them**:\n\n   a. Stop Prometheus:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n   b. Identify and remove failed blocks:\n   ```bash\n   for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     failed=$(jq '.compaction.failed' \"$d\" 2>/dev/null)\n     if [ \"$failed\" = \"true\" ]; then\n       blockdir=$(dirname \"$d\")\n       echo \"Removing failed block: $blockdir\"\n       rm -rf \"$blockdir\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n   c. Clean up temporary directories:\n   ```bash\n   find /prometheus-data/tsdb -name \".tmp-for-*\" -type d -delete\n   ```\n\n   d. Start Prometheus:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n3. **If no failed blocks, restart compaction service**:\n\n   a. Restart Prometheus:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n\n   # Watch startup logs\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|reload\"\n   ```\n\n   b. Force immediate compaction by temporarily increasing log verbosity (optional):\n   ```bash\n   # Add to Prometheus config temporarily\n   # global:\n   #   log_level: debug\n   # Then restart\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor recovery** (10-15 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Watch compaction attempts\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | \\\n     grep \"compactions_total\\|compactions_failed\"'\n\n   # Expected: compactions_total should increment\n   # If compactions_failed still increasing: proceed to step 5\n   ```\n\n5. **If compaction still fails, check for resource constraints**:\n\n   a. Memory availability:\n   ```bash\n   free -h\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep | awk '{print $6, $11}'\n   ```\n\n   b. Disk I/O:\n   ```bash\n   iostat -x 1 5  # Watch %util and iowait\n   ```\n\n   c. If constrained, restart with more resources or manual cleanup:\n   ```bash\n   # Delete some blocks manually to reduce compaction load\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/tsdb/$(ls /prometheus-data/tsdb | head -1)/\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n6. **Verify final state** (2 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Confirm compactions are progressing\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n   # Should NOT have \"compactions_failed\" increasing\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Alert on `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` > 0 for 5 minutes\n- Regularly monitor `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` (if > 100, compaction is behind)\n- Schedule periodic restarts during low-traffic windows\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Objective:** Remove corrupted block and allow Prometheus to recover gracefully.\n\n**Steps:**\n\n1. **Identify the corrupted block** (3 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # From logs\n   grep -i \"corrupted block\\|error.*block.*read\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | head -5\n\n   # Extract ULID (26 hex characters)\n   # Example: \"corrupted block 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"\n   BLOCK_ULID=\"01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"\n   ```\n\n2. **Verify it's truly corrupted**:\n   ```bash\n   # Try to dump the block\n   promtool tsdb dump /prometheus-data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ULID 2>&1 | head -50\n\n   # If errors like \"unable to read index\" or \"checksum mismatch\": it's corrupted\n   ```\n\n3. **Check if block is still actively used**:\n   ```bash\n   # Find the block's time range\n   jq '.minTime, .maxTime' /prometheus-data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ULID/meta.json\n\n   # If maxTime is old (older than 1 week): safe to delete\n   # If recent: may lose recent data\n   ```\n\n4. **Stop Prometheus before deletion**:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Delete the corrupted block**:\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ULID/\n   echo \"Deleted corrupted block: $BLOCK_ULID\"\n   ```\n\n6. **Clean up temporary blocks**:\n   ```bash\n   # Find and remove any tmp-for-* directories\n   find /prometheus-data/tsdb -name \".tmp-for-*\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null\n   find /prometheus-data/tsdb -name \".tmp-for-deletion\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null\n   ```\n\n7. **Start Prometheus**:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Watch for WAL/WBL repair if needed\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"repair\\|reload\"\n   ```\n\n8. **Verify recovery**:\n   ```bash\n   sleep 30\n\n   # Check for new corruption errors\n   grep -i \"corrupted\\|error\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -5\n\n   # Should be empty or unrelated\n\n   # Verify block loading works\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n   # Should show a reasonable number (not 0, not dramatically different)\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Use ext4/XFS with `data=ordered` mode to prevent corruption\n- Enable and monitor `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total`\n- Verify block checksums periodically:\n  ```bash\n  for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/; do\n    promtool tsdb inspect \"$(dirname $d)\" >/dev/null 2>&1 || echo \"Error: $d\"\n  done\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Objective:** Prevent OOM by reducing block compaction load or increasing memory.\n\n**Steps:**\n\n1. **Verify OOM occurred**:\n   ```bash\n   # Check system logs\n   dmesg | tail -20 | grep -i \"oom\\|killed\"\n\n   # Check Prometheus logs (if it logged before crash)\n   grep -i \"memory\\|out of memory\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -5\n   ```\n\n2. **Assess available memory**:\n   ```bash\n   # Get total memory\n   free -h\n\n   # Get Prometheus memory limit (if containerized)\n   docker inspect <container> | grep Memory  # Docker\n   kubectl describe pod <pod> | grep -A2 limits  # Kubernetes\n   ```\n\n3. **Identify problematic blocks** (Option A: shrink blocks):\n\n   a. List blocks by series count:\n   ```bash\n   for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     numSeries=$(jq '.stats.numSeries' \"$d\")\n     echo \"$(jq -r '.ulid' $d): $numSeries series\"\n   done | sort -t: -k2 -rn | head -5\n   ```\n\n   b. If any block has >1M series, it may cause OOM during compaction.\n\n   c. Manually delete the largest old block:\n   ```bash\n   LARGEST_BLOCK=$(for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do \\\n     jq -r '.ulid + \":\" + (.stats.numSeries|tostring)' \"$d\"; done | \\\n     sort -t: -k2 -rn | head -1 | cut -d: -f1)\n\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/tsdb/$LARGEST_BLOCK/\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Option B: Disable overlapping (vertical) compaction** (if enabled):\n\n   a. Edit Prometheus startup script:\n   ```bash\n   vi /etc/default/prometheus\n   # Or add to systemd service file:\n   # ExecStart=/usr/bin/prometheus --storage.tsdb.enable-overlapping-compaction=false\n   ```\n\n   b. Restart:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n   c. Overlapping compaction is more memory-intensive; disabling it reduces OOM risk.\n\n5. **Option C: Increase available memory**:\n\n   a. If containerized:\n   ```bash\n   # Docker: update docker-compose or docker run with -m flag\n   # Example: -m 8g for 8GB limit\n\n   # Kubernetes: update resources.limits.memory\n   kubectl set resources pod <pod> --limits=memory=8Gi\n   ```\n\n   b. If systemd service, increase cgroup limit:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl edit prometheus\n   # Add section:\n   # [Service]\n   # MemoryLimit=8G\n   ```\n\n   c. Restart:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n6. **Monitor compaction without OOM**:\n   ```bash\n   # Watch memory during compaction\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep | awk \"{print \\$6}\"'\n\n   # Should not exceed available memory by >10%\n   ```\n\n7. **Verify stability**:\n   ```bash\n   # Run for 30 minutes, observe no OOM kills\n   sleep 1800\n   dmesg | tail -5  # Should not show OOM kill\n\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep compactions\n   # Should show regular increments\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Set Prometheus memory limit to 60% of available system RAM\n- Monitor memory usage: `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes` + RSS usage\n- Reduce `MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize` if compaction memory is consistently high:\n  ```bash\n  # Default: 512MB, reduce to 256MB for memory-constrained systems\n  --storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size=268435456  # 256MB in bytes\n  ```\n- Alert on memory usage > 75% of limit\n\n---\n\n## 5. Overview\n\n### What is TSDB Compaction?\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction in Prometheus is the process of merging and optimizing disk-based time series blocks. As Prometheus ingests data, the in-memory \"Head\" block accumulates samples. When the Head reaches a configured time threshold (default: 2 hours), it is persisted to disk as a new block. Compaction then:\n\n1. **Merges overlapping blocks** into larger, more efficient blocks\n2. **Removes tombstoned (deleted) series** from blocks\n3. **Reorganizes data** to improve query performance\n4. **Manages disk space** by consolidating multiple small blocks into fewer larger ones\n\n### Block Structure and Levels\n\nPrometheus uses a **leveled compaction strategy**:\n\n- **Level 0**: Head blocks persisted from in-memory data (time range: typically 2 hours)\n- **Level 1+**: Progressively larger blocks created by merging smaller blocks\n\nBlock ranges grow exponentially (e.g., 2h → 10h → 50h → 250h) to maintain balanced query performance and retention efficiency.\n\n### When Compaction Is Triggered\n\nCompaction is initiated in two ways:\n\n#### 1. Time-Based (Periodic, Primary)\n- **Trigger**: Every 1 minute, the background compaction loop (`tsdb/db.go:995`) checks if the Head is compactable\n- **Condition**: Head block age ≥ half of configured `MinBlockDuration` (default: 1 hour)\n- **Code reference**: `tsdb/db.go:1162-1188`\n\n#### 2. Sample-Based (Append-Time, Secondary)\n- **Trigger**: When appenders commit samples after Head becomes \"compactable\"\n- **Condition**: Head block time range exceeds threshold\n- **Code reference**: `tsdb/db.go:1115-1127` (dbAppender.Commit)\n\n#### 3. Tombstone-Based (Cleanup)\n- **Trigger**: When a block has >5% tombstones OR all samples are deleted\n- **Condition**: Automatic selection during Plan phase\n- **Code reference**: `tsdb/compact.go:270-284`\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\n#### **Compaction Execution Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total number of completed compactions | Increasing—should increment regularly |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions attempted (may fail) | Should track with `compactions_total` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Number of failed compaction attempts | **Alert if > 0 in 1h** |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Compactions skipped (auto-compaction disabled) | Monitor; expected if compaction is disabled |\n\n#### **Compaction Duration and Performance**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Wall-clock time to complete compaction | **Alert if p99 > block_range** |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Final chunk sizes during compaction | Monitor for anomalies in distribution |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk after compaction | Monitor; indicates compression efficiency |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time range of chunks post-compaction | Monitor for fragmentation |\n\n#### **Vertical (Overlapping) Compaction**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block merges | Monitor for frequency; high frequency = many overlaps |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | 1 if block is being written, 0 otherwise | **Alert if stuck at 1 for > 5min** |\n\n#### **Block and Retention Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of currently loaded blocks | Increasing = blocks not being deleted |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total disk space used by blocks | Monitor for exceeding max disk capacity |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Configured max bytes to retain | Compare with `storage_blocks_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds` | Gauge | Configured retention duration (seconds) | Reference for time-based cleanup |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted by time-based retention | Increasing = old blocks cleaned up |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted by size-based retention | Increasing = disk limit enforced |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to clean tombstones from blocks | Monitor for unusual delays |\n\n### Sample Alert Rules\n\n```yaml\n# High-severity: Compaction is failing\n- alert: TSDBCompactionFailures\n  expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[1h]) > 0\n  for: 5m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB compaction failing on {{ $labels.instance }}\"\n    description: \"{{ $value }} compaction failures in the last hour\"\n\n# Medium-severity: Compaction is slower than block range\n- alert: TSDBCompactionSlowdown\n  expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, rate(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > on(instance) prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds / 24\n  for: 10m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB compaction is taking too long on {{ $labels.instance }}\"\n\n# Medium-severity: Block population is stuck\n- alert: TSDBBlockPopulatingStuck\n  expr: prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1\n  for: 5m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB block population stuck on {{ $labels.instance }}\"\n\n# High-severity: Disk space exhaustion imminent\n- alert: TSDBStorageNearLimit\n  expr: prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes / prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes > 0.9\n  for: 5m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB storage is at {{ $value | humanizePercentage }} of configured limit\"\n```\n\n### Distinguishing Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Healthy Compaction Indicators:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` incrementing every 1-10 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` < block time range (e.g., < 2h for 2h blocks)\n- No increase in `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` cycles between 1 and 0 (not stuck at 1)\n\n**Stuck Compaction Indicators:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` = 1 for > 5 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` increasing without completion\n- Error logs: \"compaction failed\" with increasing frequency (backoff grows: 1s → 2s → 4s → ... → 1m)\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes and Diagnostics\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Logs: `Failed to write 'Deletable' to meta file after compaction` or `remove tmp folder after failed compaction: no space left on device`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` reaches or exceeds `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes`\n- New samples rejected with I/O errors\n- Prometheus unable to create new blocks\n\n**Root Cause:**\n- Compaction requires temporary disk space to write the new merged block before deleting source blocks\n- If available free space < new block size, the write fails\n- Retention cleanup not keeping pace with ingestion rate\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check disk usage:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /prometheus-data/\n   du -sh /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n   ```\n\n2. Check current block sizes:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data/tsdb/ | head -50\n   ```\n\n3. Examine Prometheus metrics:\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\n   ```\n\n4. Review logs for specific error:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"compaction\\|disk\\|space\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -100\n   ```\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Compaction write failure: `tsdb/compact.go:606-718` (write function)\n- Temporary file handling: `tsdb/db.go:1133-1212` (Compact method)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` continuously increasing\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` not incrementing\n- Logs show backoff: \"compaction failed\" errors with exponential wait times (1s, 2s, 4s, ..., 60s)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1\n- Queries slow down due to many small blocks being queried\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` high and increasing\n\n**Root Cause:**\n- Failed block opens during compaction (corrupted metadata)\n- Mutex/locking contention during reloadBlocks\n- Insufficient memory for merging large blocks\n- Compaction plan selects blocks with `Failed` flag (prevents further compaction)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Check compaction error messages:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"failed\\|panic\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n2. Verify block integrity:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data/tsdb/ 2>&1 | grep -i \"failed\\|corrupt\\|error\"\n   ```\n\n3. List blocks and check for `Failed` status:\n   ```bash\n   ls -la /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n   for block in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     echo \"=== $block ===\"\n     jq '.compaction.failed' \"$block\"\n   done\n   ```\n\n4. Monitor block loading during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   watch -n 1 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded'\n   ```\n\n5. Check for \"reloadBlocks\" errors in logs:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"reloadBlocks\\|reload blocks\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Backoff logic: `tsdb/db.go:982-1027` (run loop with exponential backoff)\n- Compaction with failure detection: `tsdb/compact.go:305-310` (selectDirs skips blocks with Failed flag)\n- Block opening: `tsdb/compact.go:444-487` (Compact method)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Logs: `Corrupted block` or `open index reader for block ... error`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Specific blocks in `/prometheus-data/tsdb/` listed as corrupted\n- Queries fail with \"block not found\" or index read errors\n- Prometheus startup slow (repairing WAL/WBL during init)\n\n**Root Cause:**\n- Incomplete block writes (Prometheus crash during compaction)\n- Disk corruption (bitflips, filesystem errors)\n- Incompatible index/chunk format after upgrades\n- Orphaned blocks from failed compaction with temporary directory not cleaned up\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Identify corrupted blocks:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"corrupted block\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -o \"[a-z0-9]\\{26\\}\"\n   ```\n\n2. Inspect block metadata:\n   ```bash\n   # For each problematic ULID:\n   jq . /prometheus-data/tsdb/{ULID}/meta.json\n   ```\n\n3. Check block compaction status:\n   ```bash\n   jq '.compaction' /prometheus-data/tsdb/{ULID}/meta.json\n   ```\n\n4. Validate block with promtool:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /prometheus-data/tsdb/{ULID} > /tmp/dump.txt 2>&1\n   head -20 /tmp/dump.txt  # Check for errors\n   ```\n\n5. Review startup logs for WAL repair:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"repair\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Corruption detection: `tsdb/db.go:1440-1478` (reloadBlocks detects corrupted blocks)\n- Block opening with error handling: `tsdb/compact.go:475-481`\n- WAL repair on startup: `tsdb/db.go:918-933`\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Logs: `fatal error: runtime: out of memory`\n- Process receives SIGKILL or OOM killer signal\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1 before crashing\n- Memory usage spikes during compaction and never released\n- System load increases dramatically during failed compaction attempt\n\n**Root Cause:**\n- Block series count too high for available memory\n- Memory not released after closing block readers\n- Chunk pool exhaustion (too many chunks in flight)\n- Symbol table or index reader holding excessive memory\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. Monitor memory usage during compaction:\n   ```bash\n   # Before triggering compaction, start monitoring:\n   watch -n 0.5 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep | awk \"{print \\$6}\"'\n\n   # Or use Go metrics (requires pprof):\n   curl http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/heap > /tmp/heap.prof\n   go tool pprof /tmp/heap.prof\n   (pprof) top10  # Show top memory consumers\n   ```\n\n2. Check configured memory limits:\n   ```bash\n   # Check cgroup limits (container/Kubernetes):\n   cat /sys/fs/cgroup/memory/memory.limit_in_bytes\n\n   # Check Prometheus flags:\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -o \"\\-\\-storage.*\"\n   ```\n\n3. Examine block sizes before compaction:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data/tsdb/ | head -20\n   # Look for blocks with high series/chunk counts\n   ```\n\n4. Review logs for memory warnings:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"memory\\|heap\\|gc\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n**Code Reference:**\n- Memory allocation during compaction: `tsdb/compact.go:729-875` (PopulateBlock)\n- Chunk pool management: `tsdb/compact.go:77-87` (LeveledCompactor with chunkPool)\n- Symbol iteration: `tsdb/compact.go:803-810`\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery Procedure 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Objective:** Free disk space so compaction can resume and proceed normally.\n\n**Steps:**\n\n1. **Assess the situation** (2 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Check available space\n   df -h /prometheus-data/\n\n   # Get current block usage\n   du -sh /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n\n   # Get configured retention\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit\n   ```\n\n2. **Option A: Reduce retention period** (5 minutes, fastest):\n\n   a. Stop Prometheus:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n   b. Edit Prometheus config to reduce `--storage.tsdb.retention.time`:\n   ```bash\n   # Current: e.g., 30 days\n   # Reduce to: e.g., 7 days\n   vi /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n   ```\n\n   c. Start Prometheus (it will cleanup old blocks on startup):\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Monitor cleanup:\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"retention\"\n   ```\n\n   d. Verify recovery:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /prometheus-data/\n   # Should show freed space within 2 minutes\n   ```\n\n3. **Option B: Manual block deletion** (if Option A is insufficient):\n\n   a. List blocks by age:\n   ```bash\n   ls -ltr /prometheus-data/tsdb/ | tail -20\n   ```\n\n   b. Identify and delete old blocks (keep at least 3 recent blocks):\n   ```bash\n   # List all blocks with their max time\n   for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/; do\n     maxtime=$(jq .maxTime \"$d/meta.json\" 2>/dev/null)\n     echo \"$(basename $d): $maxtime\"\n   done | sort -t: -k2 -n\n\n   # Delete blocks older than X (be cautious)\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/tsdb/{OLDEST_ULID}/\n   ```\n\n   c. Restart Prometheus to re-index:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor compaction resumption** (5-10 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for compaction progress\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | \\\n     grep \"prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\\|prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes\"'\n\n   # Should see:\n   # - prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total increasing\n   # - prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes decreasing\n   ```\n\n5. **Verify health** (2 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Check for new failures\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep compactions_failed\n   # Should NOT increase after recovery\n\n   # Check disk space\n   df -h /prometheus-data/\n   # Should show adequate free space (>20% of volume recommended)\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Set `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` with 30% buffer headroom\n- Monitor `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` and alert at 80% of limit\n- Schedule regular reviews of retention policy\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Objective:** Unblock compaction by removing failed blocks or restarting the service.\n\n**Steps:**\n\n1. **Identify the root cause** (5 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Check for failed blocks in metadata\n   for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     failed=$(jq '.compaction.failed' \"$d\" 2>/dev/null)\n     if [ \"$failed\" = \"true\" ]; then\n       echo \"Failed block: $(dirname $d)\"\n     fi\n   done\n\n   # Check for specific errors\n   grep -i \"failed\\|corrupt\\|panic\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -20\n   ```\n\n2. **If failed blocks exist, clear them**:\n\n   a. Stop Prometheus:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n   b. Identify and remove failed blocks:\n   ```bash\n   for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     failed=$(jq '.compaction.failed' \"$d\" 2>/dev/null)\n     if [ \"$failed\" = \"true\" ]; then\n       blockdir=$(dirname \"$d\")\n       echo \"Removing failed block: $blockdir\"\n       rm -rf \"$blockdir\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n   c. Clean up temporary directories:\n   ```bash\n   find /prometheus-data/tsdb -name \".tmp-for-*\" -type d -delete\n   ```\n\n   d. Start Prometheus:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n3. **If no failed blocks, restart compaction service**:\n\n   a. Restart Prometheus:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n\n   # Watch startup logs\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|reload\"\n   ```\n\n   b. Force immediate compaction by temporarily increasing log verbosity (optional):\n   ```bash\n   # Add to Prometheus config temporarily\n   # global:\n   #   log_level: debug\n   # Then restart\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor recovery** (10-15 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Watch compaction attempts\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | \\\n     grep \"compactions_total\\|compactions_failed\"'\n\n   # Expected: compactions_total should increment\n   # If compactions_failed still increasing: proceed to step 5\n   ```\n\n5. **If compaction still fails, check for resource constraints**:\n\n   a. Memory availability:\n   ```bash\n   free -h\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep | awk '{print $6, $11}'\n   ```\n\n   b. Disk I/O:\n   ```bash\n   iostat -x 1 5  # Watch %util and iowait\n   ```\n\n   c. If constrained, restart with more resources or manual cleanup:\n   ```bash\n   # Delete some blocks manually to reduce compaction load\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/tsdb/$(ls /prometheus-data/tsdb | head -1)/\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n6. **Verify final state** (2 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # Confirm compactions are progressing\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n   # Should NOT have \"compactions_failed\" increasing\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Alert on `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` > 0 for 5 minutes\n- Regularly monitor `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` (if > 100, compaction is behind)\n- Schedule periodic restarts during low-traffic windows\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Objective:** Remove corrupted block and allow Prometheus to recover gracefully.\n\n**Steps:**\n\n1. **Identify the corrupted block** (3 minutes):\n   ```bash\n   # From logs\n   grep -i \"corrupted block\\|error.*block.*read\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | head -5\n\n   # Extract ULID (26 hex characters)\n   # Example: \"corrupted block 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"\n   BLOCK_ULID=\"01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"\n   ```\n\n2. **Verify it's truly corrupted**:\n   ```bash\n   # Try to dump the block\n   promtool tsdb dump /prometheus-data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ULID 2>&1 | head -50\n\n   # If errors like \"unable to read index\" or \"checksum mismatch\": it's corrupted\n   ```\n\n3. **Check if block is still actively used**:\n   ```bash\n   # Find the block's time range\n   jq '.minTime, .maxTime' /prometheus-data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ULID/meta.json\n\n   # If maxTime is old (older than 1 week): safe to delete\n   # If recent: may lose recent data\n   ```\n\n4. **Stop Prometheus before deletion**:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Delete the corrupted block**:\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/tsdb/$BLOCK_ULID/\n   echo \"Deleted corrupted block: $BLOCK_ULID\"\n   ```\n\n6. **Clean up temporary blocks**:\n   ```bash\n   # Find and remove any tmp-for-* directories\n   find /prometheus-data/tsdb -name \".tmp-for-*\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null\n   find /prometheus-data/tsdb -name \".tmp-for-deletion\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null\n   ```\n\n7. **Start Prometheus**:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Watch for WAL/WBL repair if needed\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"repair\\|reload\"\n   ```\n\n8. **Verify recovery**:\n   ```bash\n   sleep 30\n\n   # Check for new corruption errors\n   grep -i \"corrupted\\|error\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -5\n\n   # Should be empty or unrelated\n\n   # Verify block loading works\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n   # Should show a reasonable number (not 0, not dramatically different)\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Use ext4/XFS with `data=ordered` mode to prevent corruption\n- Enable and monitor `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total`\n- Verify block checksums periodically:\n  ```bash\n  for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/; do\n    promtool tsdb inspect \"$(dirname $d)\" >/dev/null 2>&1 || echo \"Error: $d\"\n  done\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Objective:** Prevent OOM by reducing block compaction load or increasing memory.\n\n**Steps:**\n\n1. **Verify OOM occurred**:\n   ```bash\n   # Check system logs\n   dmesg | tail -20 | grep -i \"oom\\|killed\"\n\n   # Check Prometheus logs (if it logged before crash)\n   grep -i \"memory\\|out of memory\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -5\n   ```\n\n2. **Assess available memory**:\n   ```bash\n   # Get total memory\n   free -h\n\n   # Get Prometheus memory limit (if containerized)\n   docker inspect <container> | grep Memory  # Docker\n   kubectl describe pod <pod> | grep -A2 limits  # Kubernetes\n   ```\n\n3. **Identify problematic blocks** (Option A: shrink blocks):\n\n   a. List blocks by series count:\n   ```bash\n   for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do\n     numSeries=$(jq '.stats.numSeries' \"$d\")\n     echo \"$(jq -r '.ulid' $d): $numSeries series\"\n   done | sort -t: -k2 -rn | head -5\n   ```\n\n   b. If any block has >1M series, it may cause OOM during compaction.\n\n   c. Manually delete the largest old block:\n   ```bash\n   LARGEST_BLOCK=$(for d in /prometheus-data/tsdb/*/meta.json; do \\\n     jq -r '.ulid + \":\" + (.stats.numSeries|tostring)' \"$d\"; done | \\\n     sort -t: -k2 -rn | head -1 | cut -d: -f1)\n\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   rm -rf /prometheus-data/tsdb/$LARGEST_BLOCK/\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Option B: Disable overlapping (vertical) compaction** (if enabled):\n\n   a. Edit Prometheus startup script:\n   ```bash\n   vi /etc/default/prometheus\n   # Or add to systemd service file:\n   # ExecStart=/usr/bin/prometheus --storage.tsdb.enable-overlapping-compaction=false\n   ```\n\n   b. Restart:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n   c. Overlapping compaction is more memory-intensive; disabling it reduces OOM risk.\n\n5. **Option C: Increase available memory**:\n\n   a. If containerized:\n   ```bash\n   # Docker: update docker-compose or docker run with -m flag\n   # Example: -m 8g for 8GB limit\n\n   # Kubernetes: update resources.limits.memory\n   kubectl set resources pod <pod> --limits=memory=8Gi\n   ```\n\n   b. If systemd service, increase cgroup limit:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl edit prometheus\n   # Add section:\n   # [Service]\n   # MemoryLimit=8G\n   ```\n\n   c. Restart:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n6. **Monitor compaction without OOM**:\n   ```bash\n   # Watch memory during compaction\n   watch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep | awk \"{print \\$6}\"'\n\n   # Should not exceed available memory by >10%\n   ```\n\n7. **Verify stability**:\n   ```bash\n   # Run for 30 minutes, observe no OOM kills\n   sleep 1800\n   dmesg | tail -5  # Should not show OOM kill\n\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep compactions\n   # Should show regular increments\n   ```\n\n**Prevention:**\n- Set Prometheus memory limit to 60% of available system RAM\n- Monitor memory usage: `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes` + RSS usage\n- Reduce `MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize` if compaction memory is consistently high:\n  ```bash\n  # Default: 512MB, reduce to 256MB for memory-constrained systems\n  --storage.tsdb.max-block-chunk-segment-size=268435456  # 256MB in bytes\n  ```\n- Alert on memory usage > 75% of limit\n\n---\n\n## 5. Code Reference\n\n### Core Compaction Files\n\n#### `tsdb/db.go`\n- **Line 982-1027**: Main compaction loop (`run` method) with 1-minute trigger and exponential backoff\n- **Line 1008-1022**: Compaction invocation with backoff on failure\n- **Line 1115-1127**: Append-time compaction triggering (`dbAppender.Commit`)\n- **Line 1133-1212**: Primary `Compact()` method orchestrating head and block compaction\n- **Line 1357-1396**: `compactBlocks()` method for multi-block compaction\n- **Line 1440-1478**: `reloadBlocks()` with corruption detection\n\n#### `tsdb/compact.go`\n- **Line 77-97**: `CompactorMetrics` struct defining all compaction metrics\n- **Line 222-286**: `Plan()` method selecting blocks for compaction, including tombstone cleanup\n- **Line 305-310**: Failed block detection (blocks with `Failed` flag skipped)\n- **Line 444-537**: `Compact()` method with error handling and `setCompactionFailed()` call\n- **Line 606-718**: `write()` method creating new block, with disk space handling\n- **Line 729-875**: `PopulateBlock()` merging series and chunks from multiple blocks\n\n#### `tsdb/block.go`\n- **Line 162-179**: `BlockMeta` structure with compaction info\n- **Line 196-212**: `BlockMetaCompaction` tracking compaction history and failures\n- **Line 456-459**: `setCompactionFailed()` marking block as failed in metadata\n\n### Metrics Instrumentation\n\n- **tsdb/compact.go:89-151**: Complete `CompactorMetrics` initialization with all 7 metrics\n- **tsdb/db.go:244-363**: `dbMetrics` with retention and block loading metrics\n\n### Failure Handling\n\n- **tsdb/db.go:1133-1212**: Compact() with defer tracking failures\n- **tsdb/compact.go:526-537**: Setting `Failed` flag on source blocks on error\n- **tsdb/db.go:918-933**: WAL/WBL corruption detection and repair on startup\n\n---\n\n## 6. Additional Resources\n\n### Promtool Commands for Investigation\n\n```bash\n# Inspect all blocks\npromtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n\n# Dump a specific block's contents\npromtool tsdb dump /prometheus-data/tsdb/{ULID}\n\n# Analyze block efficiency\npromtool tsdb analyze /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n\n# Clean tombstones from a specific block (creates new block)\npromtool tsdb clean-tombstones /prometheus-data/tsdb/\n```\n\n### Logs to Monitor\n\n- **Startup**: \"Successfully repaired WAL/WBL\" → WAL corruption occurred\n- **Compaction**: \"compact blocks\" → normal, included source blocks and time range\n- **Failures**: \"compaction failed\" → investigate error reason\n- **Cleanup**: \"Found and deleted tmp block dir\" → recovery from crash\n- **Corruption**: \"corrupted block\" → immediate action needed\n\n### Key Configuration Parameters\n\n```yaml\n# Prometheus startup flags:\n--storage.tsdb.path /prometheus-data/tsdb/          # Chunk segment size\n--web.enable-lifecycle                              # Enable /-/reload for config reloads\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary Decision Tree\n\n```\nAre compactions failing?\n├─ YES: Check prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total\n│  ├─ Disk space exhaustion error?\n│  │  └─ → Reduce retention period or manually delete old blocks\n│  │\n│  ├─ Block corruption error?\n│  │  └─ → Delete corrupted block and restart\n│  │\n│  ├─ Memory error?\n│  │  └─ → Reduce block sizes or increase available RAM\n│  │\n│  └─ \"Failed\" blocks in compaction plan?\n│     └─ → Delete blocks with compaction.failed=true\n│\n└─ NO: Compactions are healthy\n   └─ Monitor prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds\n      └─ Should not exceed block time range for more than 10 consecutive minutes\n```\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
